Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: books\\ \tt RIGHT: jacket\\ \tt TOP: cat\\ \tt BOTTOM: sunflower\\ \tt CENTER: plate\\ \tt NORTHWEST: saucepan\\ \tt NORTHEAST: horse\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: mug\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: pineapple\\ \tt HERE: cobalt\\ \tt THERE: tank top\\ \tt NOWHERE: papaya\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: jackfruit\\ \tt INSIDE: chalk\\ \tt OUTSIDE: daffodil\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <one sentence>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <one sentence>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start. 
	  } 
	   } 
	   }
